# Purgatorio - Canto 5

### 1 Io era già da quell’ ombre partito,

**gemini1-it**
- **gemini1-en**: I had already departed from those shadows,
- **gemini1-ja**: 私はすでにあの影の中から出発し、

### 2 e seguitava l’orme del mio duca,

**gemini1-it**
- **gemini1-en**: and was following the footsteps of my guide,
- **gemini1-ja**: 私の案内人の足跡をたどっていた、

### 3 quando di retro a me, drizzando ’l dito,

**gemini1-it**
- **gemini1-en**: when from behind me, pointing her finger,
- **gemini1-ja**: すると私の後ろで、指を立てて、

**gemma3-it**
- **gemma3-en**: when behind me, raising his finger,
- **gemma3-ja**: 私の背後で、指を指して、
<table>

### 19 Che potea io ridir, se non «Io vegno»?

### 45 «però pur va, e in andando ascolta».

### 51 deh, perché vai? deh, perché non t’arresti?

**gemini1-it**
- **gemini1-en**: oh, why do you go on? Oh, why don't you stop?
- **gemini1-ja**: ああ、なぜ行くのか？ああ、なぜ立ち止まらないのか？

### 63 di mondo in mondo cercar mi si face».

### 77 quel da Esti il fé far, che m’avea in ira

### 82 Corsi al palude, e le cannucce e ’l braco

**gemini1-it**
- **gemini1-en**: I ran to the marsh, and the reeds and the mud
- **gemini1-ja**: 私は沼地に駆け込み、葦と泥が

**gemma3-it**
- **gemma3-en**: I ran to the marsh, and the reeds and the bramble

### 103 Io dirò vero, e tu ’l ridì tra ’ vivi:

**gemini1-it**
- **gemini1-en**: I will tell the truth, and you repeat it among the living:
- **gemini1-ja**: 私は真実を語ろう、そしてあなたはそれを生者の間に伝えなさい。

**gemma3-it**
- **gemma3-en**: I will tell the truth, and you repeat it among the living:
- **gemma3-ja**: 私は真実を言うだろう、そしてあなたは生者たちの間でそれを言い返す：

<tr><th>Derived</th><td>Latin</td><td>Latin</td><td>Latin</td><td>Latin</td><td>Latin</td><td>Latin</td><td>Latin</td><td>Latin</td><td>Latin</td></tr>

**gptoss-it**
- **gptoss-en**: I will say true, and you will laugh it among the living:  
- **gptoss-ja**: 私は真実を言う、そしてあなたはそれを生きている者たちの間で言い直す：

### 105 gridava: “O tu del ciel, perché mi privi?

**gemini1-it**
- **gemini1-en**: cried out: "O you from heaven, why do you deprive me?
- **gemini1-ja**: 「天国の者よ、なぜ私から奪うのか？」と叫んだ。

**gemma3-it**
- **gemma3-en**: cried out: “O you from heaven, why do you deprive me?
- **gemma3-ja**: 叫んだ。「おお、天の者よ、なぜ私から奪うのか？

### 119 la pioggia cadde, e a’ fossati venne

### 121 e come ai rivi grandi si convenne,

**gemini1-it**
- **gemini1-en**: and as was fitting for the great streams,
- **gemini1-ja**: そして大きな川にふさわしく、

**gemma3-it**
- **gemma3-en**: and as to the great rivers it converged,
- **gemma3-ja**: そして大きな川に集まるように、

### 134 Siena mi fé, disfecemi Maremma:
